1936.05.11

Conference of Senior Local Administrative Personnel Held Opening Ceremony Yesterday Morning After Paying Respects at the Mausoleum; President Chiang Presided, Reporting the Significance of the Meeting; Civil Affairs, Public Security, and Education Groups Held Separate Meetings in the Afternoon 1

(Nanjing) The conference of senior local administrative personnel from ten provinces opened on the morning of the 10th. At 8:00 AM, the entire group paid respects at the mausoleum. At 10:00 AM, the opening ceremony was held at the Lixingshe. President Chiang himself came to deliver instructions. Chairman Yang Yongtai of Hubei also rushed to attend at noon. President Chiang hosted a banquet for all attendees at noon. In the afternoon, civil affairs, public security, and education groups held review meetings. Jiang Tingfu chaired the civil affairs group, Weng Wenhao chaired the public security group, and Duan Xipeng chaired the education group, reviewing proposals. Review will continue on the 11th, morning and afternoon. (Special dispatch on the 10th)

(Nanjing) To inquire about the local administrative situation in various provinces, President Chiang, in addition to scheduling meetings with the chairmen of five provinces, also scheduled meetings for the 11th and 12th with the civil affairs chiefs of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, and Hubei, and in the afternoon, with the administrative inspectors of nine provinces. On the morning of the 12th, he will meet with the chiefs and inspectors of Hunan, Fujian, Henan, Shandong, and Shaanxi. (Special dispatch on the 10th)

(Nanjing) The conference of senior local administrative personnel opened on the morning of the 10th. At 8:00 AM, all attendees respectfully visited the mausoleum of the Premier, presided over by President Chiang. After the ceremony, they proceeded to respectfully view the remains. After the ceremony, they returned to the city. At 10:00 AM, the opening ceremony was held in the auditorium of the Lixingshe, chaired by President Chiang, who reported on the significance of convening the conference. He stated that the purpose of convening the conference was to understand the advantages and disadvantages of the administrative inspector system after its implementation and to seek reforms. Today, central and local administrative officials are gathered together, and he hoped that they would fully discuss various issues to improve administrative efficiency. Subsequently, Weng Wenhao reported on the preparations for the conference and decided on the personnel and chairmen for the group meetings. The meeting adjourned at noon, and President Chiang immediately hosted a banquet at the Lixingshe. At 2:30 PM, the civil affairs, public security, and education groups held separate meetings, chaired by Jiang Jianfu, Weng Wenhao, and Duan Xipeng, respectively. The discussions were based on the "Abstract of Opinions on the Attention to Improvement of Local Administrative Principles" and "Reference Materials for Discussion Topics." The meeting adjourned at 5:30 PM. The results of the discussions in each group will be submitted for discussion at the general meeting on the morning of the 12th. Group meetings will be held in the morning and afternoon of the 11th. In addition, the National Academic Work Advisory Office hosted a banquet for all representatives at the Lixingshe at 6:00 PM on the 10th. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 10th)

Conference Attendees

(Nanjing) Those who attended the conference of senior local administrative personnel on the morning of the 10th included guests such as Zhang Qun, Chen Shaokuan, Wu Dingchang, Chen Shuru, Yu Feipeng, Duan Xipeng, and more than a dozen others. The presidium included President Chiang, Kong Xiangxi, Chiang Tso-pin, Wang Shijie, He Yingqin, Weng Wenhao, and Jiang Tingfu. Attendees included Chen Guofu, Huang Shaoxiong, Liu Zhenhua, Xiong Shihui, Yang Yongtai, the five chairmen, Yu Jingtang, civil affairs chief of Jiangsu; Zhou Fohai, education chief; inspectors Mei Siping, Zang Qifang, Wang Gongyu, Ge Tan, Shi Kuiling, Wang Depu, Hao Guoxi, Na Hanyuan; Xu Qingfu, civil affairs chief of Zhejiang; Xu Shaodi, education chief; inspectors Wang Xianqiang, Huang Renwang, Zhao Juesheng, He Jieling, Pang Jingtang, Hu Juewei, Lu Zhongxiu, Xu Panyun; Ma Lingfu, civil affairs chief of Anhui; Yang Lian, education chief; inspectors Yang Zhongming, Gao Wenbo, Wu Tinglin, Ma Jidi, Lin Yousong, Lu Peizhang, Nan Yuejun, Wang Zhenhuai, Zeng Qian, Shi Guozhu; Wang Juefu, civil affairs chief of Jiangxi; Gan Shixu, education chief; inspectors Fu Jiang, Wei Suzhong, Li Zhengyi, Wang Youlan, Feng Jingfu, Zhou Zuofu, Shao Hongji; Ling Zhang, civil affairs chief of Hunan; Zhu Jingnong, education chief; inspectors Wei Daofeng, Yu Fanchuan, Luo Shouyi, Zhang Qixiong; Meng Guangpeng, civil affairs chief of Hubei; Cheng Qibao, education chief; inspectors Huang Gongzhu, Yang Enxi, Wang Lie, Fu Hengbo, Guan Linshu; Gao Dengting, civil affairs chief of Fujian; Zheng Zhenwen, education chief; inspectors Wang Boqiu, Lin Zhitang, Chen Yifeng, Si Lie, Zhu Xi, Shao Qiyong, Qin Zhenwen; Li Shuchun, civil affairs chief of Shandong; He Siyuan, education chief; inspectors Wang Zhaochang, Sun Zerang, Zhang Liyuan; Li Peiji, civil affairs chief of Henan; Chen Fangxian, education chief; inspectors Ruan Fancai, Zhu Jiuying, Wang Zemin, Wang Yinxi, Xu Yaping, Luo Zhen, Huang Mian, Fu Weiji, Yan Xunfu, Sheng Shiheng, Ouyang Zhen; Peng Zhaoxian, civil affairs chief of Shaanxi; Zhou Xuechang, education chief; inspectors Mao Xuzhai, Cao Guohua, Han Zhensheng, Wei Xiru, Zhang Dulun, and ninety others. Central representatives included Chen Bulei, Gan Naiguang, Xu Xiangshu, Duanmu Kai, Zhang Rui, Teng Gu, Deng Jiesong, Chen Kewen, Chen Rui, Hu Mai, Wu Jingchao, Zheng Daoru, Li Xuantiao, Sun Xiwu, Luo Junqiang, Li Pusheng, Liang Dong, Li Wan, Zhou Xiaobo, and Sun Mujia. Military Affairs Commission representatives included Liu Jianqun, Luo Gonghua, Xu Qingyu, Xu Daolin, Zhang Yiding, Li Yujiu, Gao Chuanzhu; Lei Zhen from the Ministry of Education; Gu Shusen; Li Songfeng from the Ministry of Interior; Liu Fu; Cai Pei; Gao Bingfang from the Ministry of Finance; Weng Zhiyong; Jin Baoshan from the Health Department, and thirty-four others. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 10th)

President Chiang's Instruction

(Nanjing) President Chiang's instructions at the local administrative conference on the morning of the 10th were titled "The Purpose and Key Points of the Local Administrative Conference." The original text is as follows:

"Outline" The purpose of the conference is to review the effectiveness of local administration to reform malpractices and improve efficiency. The key points of the conference are: 1. Each person should contribute as much research material as possible; 2. Deliberate on the advantages and disadvantages of current administrative laws and regulations (with special attention to the rationalization of expenditure use); 3. Close connection between local government departments; 4. Education should focus on enriching teachers and training unemployed youth; 5. The most important tasks in civil affairs are (A) improving police administration, (B) implementing land administration. It is hoped that there will be mutual learning and discussion so that this conference can achieve the most satisfactory results.

Fellow comrades, in March two years ago, we convened a conference of senior administrative personnel from various provinces in Nanchang to discuss improving local administrative matters. At that time, it was decided that such a conference could be held annually, both to hear reports from various regions and to discuss ways to improve. However, last year, I was stationed in Sichuan, and transportation was inconvenient, so I was unable to convene it. Now, the Executive Yuan has convened the chiefs and inspectors of various provincial departments to hold the second local administrative conference here. At the opening of the conference today, I would like to briefly report to you the purpose of convening the conference and the key points of discussion. Roughly speaking, the most important purpose of each of our conferences is to focus on the past year, especially the two basic aspects of local administration, namely civil affairs and education. We want to take advantage of the opportunity of this conference to report on the actual implementation and the practical experience gained by everyone, so that everyone can report, learn from each other, and jointly discuss in order to improve past shortcomings and solve current difficulties, so that local administration can be accelerated in the future. This is the purpose of our conference. As for the key points of the conference, to sum it up, there are the following items: First, the biggest purpose of our conference is to use the actual situation of our local governance and everyone's experience as materials for research, to increase the efficiency of local administration. Then, the most important basic task for all of us attending the conference is, of course, to present the actual situation of local governance and our own experiences, especially our recent special insights, as well as the difficulties encountered and the shortcomings discovered, to the conference as much as possible, so that everyone can get good materials for research. Second, regarding the various existing administrative laws and regulations, whether they are regulations or systems related to organization, personnel, or funding, can they be implemented effectively in various places? Are there any obstacles? And what is the situation of implementation? What are the advantages and disadvantages? We hope that everyone will conduct an objective review and practical research at this conference, and then consider the advantages and disadvantages to achieve perfection. Because our country is still in a difficult and creative process, especially since the situation in various places is very different, it is very difficult to apply a regulation or system universally across the country. Therefore, all laws and regulations must, under the principles established by the central government, adapt to the specific circumstances of each place, consider the advantages and disadvantages, and make various adjustments and remedies, so that they can be used flexibly and measures can be appropriate. This matter requires the conscientious discussion of all comrades attending the conference, especially regarding the funding item. Now, whether in the central or local government, it has become a very difficult problem. To solve this problem, there are only two ways: increasing revenue and reducing expenditure. However, except for the future when transportation, agriculture, mining, and related economic industries can be developed to increase revenue, it can be said that there is no source to open up based on the current situation. As for the method of reducing expenditure, the central and local governments have been paying attention to it recently. In this difficult period, everyone should, of course, try to save as much as possible, using one penny as ten. However, based on the current situation, I am afraid that the funds that can be saved in various places are also very limited. We cannot increase revenue, and it is difficult to reduce expenditure. Then, how will the problem of various expenses be solved in the future? I believe that the most important and relatively easy way to do this is to make a comprehensive calculation of existing expenditures, distinguish the essentials and the non-essentials of the cause, the relative importance, the order of urgency, and the size of the benefits that can be generated, and make reasonable adjustments to increase or decrease them. We must always shift from slow to urgent, from light to heavy, and transform the useless into the useful. I think that although the funding in various places is difficult now, if we make a detailed plan according to this principle and allocate it appropriately, we can definitely increase the efficiency of politics greatly. For example, the funding for security teams used to be the responsibility of the county itself, and it was impossible to count. Now, each province has unified it across the region or the province, which will reduce a lot of wasteful and wasted expenses compared to before. If we find a way to reorganize it in the future, I believe that we can definitely save more expenses. Now, various places spend a lot of money to support security teams. Some of them are corrupt, neither like the national defense army nor like the local army. This kind of nondescript army is of no benefit to the country and is often harmful to the local area. It should be reduced and the remaining funds should be used to handle baojia or improve the police, and its effect must be more than it is now. This is just one example. There are many other aspects that can be reduced and tightened, and the useless can be turned into useful expenses. As long as all comrades can discuss with a "public and loyal country" mind, they will definitely come up with a solution and achieve considerable results. Third, there are, of course, many reasons why the administrative efficiency of various places has not been greatly improved in recent years, and the lack of horizontal connections between the civil affairs, finance, education, and construction departments is also one of the important reasons. Each department only cares about its own affairs and cannot truly work together as a whole. We must know that a provincial government is originally a whole, so it is divided into four departments, but this is only for the convenience of work, so that each is responsible for its own responsibilities in order to promote it. In terms of spirit and cause, it is originally an inseparable whole, especially the promotion of all the work of each department and the development of the cause, which are all closely related to success or failure. Only when everyone works together can we truly do things, and it is not good to each govern its own government. Therefore, civil affairs must take into account finance, education, and construction, and education must take into account civil affairs, finance, and construction. Any department must take into account the other three departments, especially civil affairs and education, which are closely related to each other and must be in close contact with each other. Only in this way can they complement each other, and no matter what the matter is in civil affairs, finance, education, or construction, it can be done with half the effort and double the results. Therefore, although the chiefs of finance and construction departments of various provinces did not attend this conference, the civil affairs and education chiefs should also pay attention to discussing the affairs of finance and construction in various provinces. At the same time, when discussing civil affairs and education matters, they must also take into account the situation of finance and construction. All the methods for mutual assistance and cooperation between the various departments to work together as a whole in order to improve administrative efficiency, I hope that everyone will pay attention to discussing at this conference. Fourth, if we want to develop education in the future, on the one hand, we must try to popularize it in order to increase the quantity, but on the other hand, we must strive for quality improvement in order to progress. In terms of our current strength and the actual needs, we should first seek quality improvement for education, and then increase the quantity. Because the most serious problem in our country and society is not that there are too few literate citizens or educated people, but that these educated people, who account for only a very small number of the total population, have unhealthy knowledge and abilities, and most of them do not have appropriate occupations. Those who are responsible for school education and social education cannot properly guide ordinary people and school-age children who lack knowledge. Therefore, if we want to develop education, we must first improve education. If we want to improve education, we must first improve teachers, especially to train a large number of primary and secondary school teachers. If primary and secondary school teachers cannot be healthy and do not understand the purpose of education and the responsibility of teachers, our education will be useless no matter how popular it is. Moreover, bad education will spread. Under bad education, the more literate people are educated, the less our society and country will benefit. Therefore, in the future, whether it is the central government or various local governments, we must first pay attention to cultivating healthy teachers to improve education, and first be able to improve in terms of quality, and then gradually promote it in terms of quantity. Only in this way can education develop healthily, and the country can have a solid foundation. Now, many young college graduates are unemployed. These young students have all been educated by the society and the country for a long time, but they do not have the opportunity to serve the society and the country. This is really the most contradictory phenomenon and the greatest loss to the country and society. If we want to remedy this in the future, it is best for the central government or local governments to find a way to convene these unemployed college graduates and give them the necessary training so that they can become healthy primary and secondary school teachers and mentors to the people, and shoulder the basic work of various aspects of civil affairs and education in various places. This matter has infinite benefits for both the youth themselves and the society and the country, and it is not difficult to do. Now, when the post office wants to recruit postal workers and ordinary agencies record events, the monthly salary is only a dozen or twenty yuan, and there are often only two or three vacancies, but hundreds of people come to apply. This shows the difficulty of life in general and the number of unemployed students. Therefore, although we do not have a lot of funds, it is not difficult to train a large number of healthy teachers. In the next year, our primary and secondary school education is expected to increase by one-fourth in terms of quantity. We should now hurry up to train one-fourth of the primary and secondary school teachers to prepare for supplementation. In the future, we will train teachers year by year, which can gradually reduce the number of unemployed college or secondary school graduates, and gradually improve and popularize our education. How can this matter be implemented effectively to promote the benefits to the fullest? I would like to ask everyone to pay attention to research. Fifth, I believe that the most urgent things in civil affairs are two things: in the negative aspect, we must improve police administration; in the positive aspect, we must implement land administration. We know that whatever things in the world, if they are not beneficial, they are harmful. For example, the police were originally used to maintain public order and increase social welfare, which is of course very important and very beneficial. However, now the police in our country are useless and harmful. If we go to various rural areas to investigate in person, we will know that the police in many places now not only cannot maintain public order and increase welfare, but also cover up smoking, gambling, prostitution, poverty, extortion, and even collude with bandits to oppress good people, and commit all kinds of evil. Not only the police in remote areas are often like this, but also the police in big cities cannot be completely exempt. The police in various places have such bad habits on the one hand, and on the other hand, they have too little funding, so it is not easy to improve the police. Therefore, I have always believed that the police in various places with insufficient funding are absolutely useless and harmful to the people. It is best to abolish them all and replace them with baojia or groups. You have been engaged in local administrative work for a long time, and you must know that the teams in various places have the problems of the teams, the baojia have the problems of the baojia, and the local bullies have the problems of the local bullies. Among the various morbid states, especially the problems of the police are particularly numerous. How should we reduce, train, reform, and refresh them in the future so that they can fulfill the responsibilities of the police? I hope that everyone will pay special attention to research. This is the most important thing in the negative aspect of civil affairs work. As for the positive aspect, it is to implement land administration in order to solve the land problem. Everyone must know that the land problem is a fundamental problem in politics, and land administration is a basic work in politics. If land administration cannot be implemented perfectly and the land problem cannot be solved properly, political construction will not only fail, but also be impossible to promote. Everyone should not think that to implement land administration, we must first raise a lot of funds before we can proceed. If so, our land administration will not be able to proceed with anything and will never be done well. Therefore, we must regard this as a fundamental and important policy, raise a part of the most necessary funds, and try our best to implement it. At this conference, everyone should report on the situation of land administration in various provinces, refer to each other, and make a common resolution to serve as a basis for promotion in the future. The above are the few brief points that I would like to raise to you today at the opening of the conference. I hope that everyone will discuss these points carefully. It is really a rare opportunity for senior administrative personnel from ten provinces to gather together. I hope that everyone will take advantage of this opportunity to contribute their experiences and opinions as much as possible, learn from each other, and discuss with each other, so that this conference can achieve the most satisfactory results, and the administration of various places in the future can achieve the greatest progress, and we can fulfill our responsibilities and complete our mission of teaching the country and saving the people. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 10th)

Clean-Up Campaign Held in the Capital of Hebei Province 2

(Baoding) For the clean-up campaign in the capital of Hebei Province, various agencies and organizations gathered in front of the provincial government at 6:30 AM on the 10th. After Zhang Jiyong, Wan Fulin, and Zhang Yunrong explained the significance of the campaign, the chiefs of various departments and offices personally carried tools and swept the designated areas. The campaign ended at 9:00 AM. In addition, Zhang Yunrong and Li Xin inspected the discipline training of various elementary schools in Qingyuan County on the 9th, and the order was excellent. The Department of Education held a children's health campaign at the attached elementary school of Baoding Normal School on the 10th, showing knowledge slides. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 10th)

Large-Scale Smuggling of Petroleum into North China; U.S. Consulate in Tianjin Lodges Protest with Customs; More Than 31,000 Cases Arrived Last Month; U.S. Petroleum Sales Market Almost Completely Seized; Tianjin Customs Revenue Sharply Reduced 3

(Tianjin) The U.S. Consul-General in Tianjin protested to the Customs, stating that a total of 31,000 cases of smuggled gasoline and petroleum arrived last month, with a cost of $5.35 per case. The unloading locations were Yanghekou, Nandasi, Beidaihe, and Changli Liushouying in eastern Hebei. 13,000 cases have been transported from the 1st to the 9th, flooding the market. A certain petroleum company in a Tianjin concession specializes in this business, and the U.S. oil sales market has been almost completely seized. The British Consul-General will also make a similar representation. (Special dispatch on the 10th)

(Tianjin) The U.S. Consul-General has protested to the Tianjin-Qinhuangdao Customs regarding the smuggling of petroleum into North China and dumping at low prices, demanding a stop. (Special dispatch on the 10th)

(Tianjin) Armed gunboats of the Japanese Tianjin-Qinhuangdao and Zhifu Customs are seizing smuggled ships in the Bohai Bay south of the Laotieshan Cape. Eleven ships of 500 tons each have been seized so far. The Governor-General of the Kwantung Territory has protested to us through the Tianjin Consulate, alleging intrusion into public territorial waters. Negotiations are underway. (Special dispatch on the 10th)

(Tianjin) Tianjin Post Office is paying attention to inspecting parcels sent abroad, and if it finds suspected smuggled goods, it will stop sending them and hand them over to the customs for inspection. If there is no tax bill, it will be confiscated. Previously, it could receive and send 4,000 parcels per day, but now it has been reduced by half. Smugglers have probably abandoned this route. (Special dispatch on the 10th)

(Tianjin) According to Tianjin Customs statistics, the total tax revenue collected by the Customs and the tax cards at the Great Wall ports last year reached more than 41 million yuan. Due to the impact of smuggling this year, it has been reduced by as much as 20 million yuan. Although export taxes have increased by hundreds of thousands of yuan, it is far from enough to compensate. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 10th)

(Tianjin) From November last winter to the end of last month, the Tianjin-Qinhuangdao and Great Wall ports lost 20 million in customs duties due to smuggling. Although export taxes increased by hundreds of thousands, the difference is huge. (Special dispatch on the 10th)

(Tianjin) Korean laborers formed labor groups at the Qinhuangdao wharf to contract for unloading smuggled goods. Recently, Japanese laborers also formed labor groups to compete for business. On the 9th, a vicious fight broke out over the business, resulting in many casualties. The Japanese Consulate in Tianjin dispatched a large vessel, Zhongren, to investigate on the 10th. (Special dispatch on the 10th)

(Tianjin) According to Japanese investigations, from March 23 to the present, the Japanese ships transporting rayon and sugar that have been intercepted by the Customs anti-smuggling gunboats are Yurong Maru, Bianyang Maru, Fuan Maru, Dengzhou Maru, Xifu Maru, Changsheng Maru, Shoude Maru Zhoufashun, Hiruko Maru, Feihang Maru, and Xintongshun, totaling eleven ships. The places where they were seized were all 120 nautical miles south of the Laotieshan Cape in Lushun and the Customs ship lies in wait at 60–70 nautical miles between the Laotieshan Cape and Zhifu. When a ship carrying smuggled goods comes, it follows it, then speeds up to intercept it near Changli or outside Zhifu port. (Special dispatch on the 10th)

(Tianjin) Regarding smuggling in North China, a certain party stated that if the Hebei-Chahar authorities cannot follow their instructions and make some performance, and want to seek assistance in cracking down on it to achieve a complete ban, they must adapt to the current environment in North China, reduce the tax rate, or change the method of collection. Otherwise, they cannot help in any way. Xiao Xichao, an inspector from the Ministry of Finance, took the resolutions made in Tianjin and returned to the Ministry to report within days. The trip to Chahar, Shanxi, Shandong, and Suiyuan was postponed. (Special dispatch on the 10th)

(Tianjin) On the 9th and 10th, ice police intercepted several smuggled ships in the Ziya Daqing Southern Grand Canal. Japanese Consul Nagai protested again. The municipal government and customs decided to take a consistent attitude, saying that anti-smuggling is our legal action and there is nothing wrong with it. They decided to reply separately on the 11th. (Special dispatch on the 10th)

Commentary

The League of Nations at a Critical Juncture 11

— Lang

As Italian troops advance into Addis Ababa, the capital of Abyssinia, the fate of Abyssinia is about to end, and the League of Nations in Geneva has reached a final critical juncture. Since Italy launched the aggression war in East Africa on October 3 last year, the League of Nations has declared Italy an aggressor and imposed economic sanctions. Since then, the economic war against Italy by more than 50 countries has followed the Italian-Abyssinian war. Now, after seven months, the East African War has ended due to the poor equipment of Abyssinia, and the economic war against Italy by the League of Nations has not achieved significant and rapid results due to the uneven front among its member states. After the end of the East African War, will Geneva's economic war continue or stop? If it stops, it will not only show that Italy has defeated Geneva, but also that the fate of the League of Nations will end with the failure of Abyssinia. If it continues, it will be unwanted by those countries that hold pragmatism. In such a dilemma, the League of Nations has reached a final critical juncture.

Because of the serious blow Geneva has suffered, governments are now discussing how to deal with the aftermath. Some advocate reorganizing the League of Nations, deleting the provisions of Articles 10 and 16 of the Covenant, and making it purely a peaceful organization for mediating international disputes. Others still advocate continuing sanctions against Italy to maintain the last breath of the League of Nations. The British government is naturally most concerned about the future of the League of Nations, because the implementation of sanctions against Italy by the League of Nations was largely due to the power launched by the United Kingdom. Therefore, the failure of sanctions and the victory of Rome over Geneva is tantamount to the victory of Italy over the United Kingdom. Regarding the aftermath of the League of Nations, the Conservative government mostly advocates ending sanctions and reorganizing the League of Nations' organization. Prime Minister Baldwin said: "The British government, in view of the failure of collective action in the Italian-Abyssinian war, must clarify the status of the League of Nations." Foreign Secretary Eden also said in the House of Commons debate on foreign policy on the 6th: "The League of Nations' actions failed to prevent the outbreak of war before the war was waged, nor could they stop the war from proceeding after the war was waged. At most, the League of Nations only makes war more difficult and costly... The government will deal with the difficulties it encounters in a pragmatic spirit and with constructive political means." In addition, former Foreign Secretary Chamberlain and Lord Louraine in the House of Lords also advocated stopping sanctions and reorganizing the League of Nations. However, opposition party members such as Dalton and Attlee firmly advocated continuing sanctions. South African Federal Prime Minister Hertzog even advocated maintaining sanctions against Italy for several years to force Italy to make concessions. In addition, representatives of Northern European countries such as Sweden, Denmark, Norway, and the Netherlands met on the 9th and unanimously advocated observing the attitudes of Britain and France. If they cannot obtain any real and concrete results, they will consider forming a new League of Nations based on principles of justice. It is expected that the Executive Yuan, which will meet today, will discuss the Italian-Abyssinian issue, but the passage of the resolution to terminate sanctions is certainly not yet the time. However, the survival of the League of Nations will ultimately be decided in the near future.

In recent years, because aggressive imperialists have successively withdrawn from the League of Nations in Geneva, the League of Nations has become a relatively better organization for maintaining international peace. This setback is due to the lack of sincerity of major powers such as Britain and France in truly upholding the collective system. Many people hate the League of Nations because it cannot effectively help Abyssinia. In fact, the League of Nations is not a supreme government. It itself has no power. Its power is entirely based on its member states, especially the people who love peace. At a time when aggressors are complacent and the world is full of gunpowder, the establishment of a collective security system is very urgent, and the organization of the League of Nations is still an important factor in the collective security system, so it is necessary to continue to exist. However, the League of Nations has now reached a final critical juncture. How to maintain its life and enrich its power is a problem that people who love peace need to consider and solve.

Local General Budgets for Various Provinces and Cities in the 25th Year Must Be Handled in Advance, and the Review Procedures for Provincial and Municipal Budgets Will Be Shortened 12

(Nanjing) The 24th year is coming to an end, and many provinces and cities still have not submitted their local general budgets for the 23rd and 24th years to the central government through legislative procedures. It is said that the reason for the delay is that the review during previous decisions was delayed for too long. For example, at the beginning of the preparation of a provincial local general budget, the provincial government first reviewed it, and after submitting it to the Executive Yuan, it had to be reviewed again. After being forwarded to the Central Political Council, it still had to be reviewed. The Central Political Council sent it to the Directorate-General of Budgets, Accounts and Statistics for compilation, and after transferring it to the Legislative Yuan, it had to be reviewed again. In order to be cautious, each agency has undergone four decisions of review. There was once a provincial budget in which questions arose during the review, and when the province was asked to send personnel to Beijing to state their opinions, the personnel in the province had already been transferred. If this continues, it will lose the original purpose of establishing a budget system. Now the 25th year is about to begin. It is hoped that the national general budget for the 25th year can be completed according to the precedent of the 24th year before the beginning of the year, and it is still difficult to determine whether each province and city can complete the legislative procedures uniformly before the beginning of the year. In addition to instructing each province and city to handle the local general budget for that year in advance in order to comply with the spirit of the budget system, the central authorities will also find ways to shorten the review procedures for provincial and municipal budgets in order to save time and avoid delays. (10th Central News Agency Telegram)

Washington Observers: The European Situation Is Increasingly in Crisis; Conflict Over Control of the Mediterranean; A Showdown Between Britain and Italy Is Almost Inevitable 13

(Washington) Foreign policy observers here believe today that the European crisis caused by Italy's annexation of Abyssinia will be more serious than when Mussolini launched his troops to attack Abyssinia. In the future, conflicts over control of the Mediterranean will be unavoidable. Britain's need for free passage through the Suez Canal to connect with India and the East will be directly opposed to Mussolini's repeated statement that "the Mediterranean will be Italy's lake." Moreover, Britain's desire to maintain the European balance of power and maintain peace through collective security is also a cause of international tension. State Department officials stated today that they have not yet received formal notification regarding the status of Chargé d'Affaires Engert in Abyssinia, so they are unwilling to express what steps the U.S. government will take. President Roosevelt has sent a telegram to Mr. Engert, praising his spirit during difficult times and promising to recommend him for promotion. (9th National Telegram)

The League of Nations' Credibility Is Lost; Britain's Procrastination Is Misleading; Herriot Publishes an Article 14

(Paris) Édouard Herriot, leader of the Radical Socialist Party and Mayor of Lyon, recently published an article in the party's newspaper, the "Action Report," discussing the international situation. He believes that the crisis is imminent and that the League of Nations has collapsed and France has been isolated. The cause is that domestic opinions in Britain are divided, the Little Entente and the Balkan Entente countries have lost credibility and have to seek help themselves, and the dictatorial countries control everything and do not hesitate to despise the liberal countries. "On the one hand, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini annexed Abyssinia with straightforward means, and on the other hand, he prepared to listen to the League of Nations' mediation and re-participate in negotiations on collective security. What he did was to disregard everything. How can we be so ignored?" (10th Havas Telegram)

British Secretary of War Visits French and Belgian Borders to Pay Respects to the Graves of Fallen Soldiers of the European War 15

The British Secretary of State for War, Duff Cooper, and his wife, arrived in Hazebrouck, France, from England at 4:00 p.m. They immediately joined local officials to go to the public cemetery of European War soldiers in Roussonck to place flowers in front of the spirits of fallen soldiers from various countries (9,810 British, 658 French, and 223 German). Then, they went to Ypres, Belgium, to pay respects to the public cemetery of 35,000 fallen British soldiers, and are scheduled to go to Bas-Pendaele tomorrow to pay respects to the public cemetery of fallen Belgian soldiers. (9th Havas Telegram)

New Roman Imperialism; Mussolini Announces Annexation of Black Lion Country in East Africa; Italian King Gains Title of Emperor of Abyssinia; Badoglio Appointed as Foothold 16

(Rome) Tonight, amid the chiming of church bells and the sound of whistles everywhere, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini announced to 200,000 people in the Piazza Venezia that Abyssinia would be incorporated into Italian territory. When Mussolini delivered his speech, the public was so excited that almost every sentence was interrupted by cheers. Mussolini said that he had officially ordered the Abyssinian Empire to be placed under the full and complete sovereignty of Italy. Italian King Emmanuel III has added the title of Emperor of Abyssinia. Abyssinia will be ruled by a governor, and the governors of Eritrea and Somaliland will be under his control. Mussolini then announced amid thunderous cheers that General Badoglio, who had triumphed in East Africa, would be appointed Governor of Abyssinia.

Mussolini said in his speech: Italy has finally completed its empire. This is the fascist empire with the Roman seal of indestructible determination and power. This is also an empire of peace, because Italy wants to be at peace with itself and all other countries. However, if any country wants to oppose us with force, we must defend ourselves. The young generation of Italy has been painstakingly working for fourteen years for the purpose of this empire. This is the tradition of Rome, because Rome, after victory, always merges with the defeated nation, coexisting and prospering together. This brings an era in Italian history to an end and opens a great gateway to the possibilities of the future, to enter a new era. Can you be up to the task? After the crowd shouted that they could, Mussolini said again, "This cry is nothing less than a great oath before God and mankind that will never change."

Mussolini's speech did not mention the League of Nations or any countries related to Abyssinia. This is particularly noteworthy. It is expected that the Italian representative to the League of Nations, Aloisi, will refuse to discuss the Abyssinian issue at the League of Nations Administrative Council meeting on Sunday, deny that the Abyssinian representative, Mr. Monde, has the right to be a "subject" of the new empire, and will demand that he (Aloisi) be the sole representative of Abyssinia.

Tonight, before Mussolini made this historically memorable announcement, the Fascist Supreme Council met for ten minutes and the Cabinet met for three minutes to pass the annexation of Abyssinia.

Today, the people of Rome are so happy that words cannot describe it. Hours before Mussolini's announcement, people flocked to the Piazza Venezia, waiting for Mussolini's appearance, causing the streets in the city center to be blocked by vehicles. The Piazza Venezia was extremely beautiful, with all the houses decorated with electric lights, illuminating it like daytime. When Mussolini gave his speech, the Roman garrison was stationed around the Tomb of the Unknown Soldier. (9th Reuters Telegram)

Determined to Resist the World

(Rome) Italy's decision to annex Abyssinia is an act of resistance to the League of Nations and the United Kingdom and France. When the League of Nations Administrative Council meets on Monday, Abyssinia, with 350,000 square miles and 10 million people, has already been swallowed up by Italy as a fait accompli. Mussolini claimed today that Italy will defend this newly acquired territory with red blood, which shows its determination to resist the world. Now, among the titles of Italian kings, only the monarchs of Britain and Japan are comparable. Mussolini's speech lasted eleven minutes. He said, "Italians have created an empire with red blood and should make it prosperous with labor. Italy wants peace with the world and does not want war unless forced to do so. Therefore, its empire is an empire of peace, and for the people of Abyssinia, it is also an empire of culture and guidance." (9th National Telegram)

Various Countries Adopt a Reserved Attitude

(London) Authorities around the world have adopted a reserved attitude toward Mussolini's declaration on the annexation of Abyssinia. No one is making comments lightly. French political circles are not surprised, but they do not conceal that this move is unfavorable to all parties, especially Britain and France. British Foreign Secretary Eden and his entourage only said before going to Geneva, "This is what we expected." Political circles in Berlin refused to comment, saying that Germany has always maintained a neutral attitude and will not change now. The Berlin Daily said that the title of Caesar was resurrected not in Rome but in Africa. This is truly a great fantasy of fate. Mussolini's actions have brought Africa closer to Europe and will inevitably cause new problems and dangers. Geneva is speculating on the actions that various countries will take, and is focusing on Britain and France. Many people feel that although France is willing to turn a deaf ear to Italy's aggression, it also did not expect such a serious result. All the small countries are very frightened. At the same time, the Americas all believe that the United States will abide by the Stimson Non-Recognition Doctrine, as before with "Manchukuo," and refuse to recognize the new situation created by force. The American public now recognizes this as the foundation of American policy. (10th Reuters Telegram)

Rome Celebrates Enthusiastically; Citizens Cheer and Dance All Night; Military Songs and Party Songs Resonate 17

(Rome) After Prime Minister Mussolini announced the annexation of Abyssinia last night, citizens cheered and danced all night, and went to the Royal Palace to cheer and pay tribute to Italian King and Emperor of Abyssinia Emmanuel III. The king accepted the congratulations on the balcony. Celebrations were held simultaneously throughout the country. In addition, Prime Minister Mussolini received British Ambassador Grandi at the Palazzo Venezia, as well as the envoys of countries that did not participate in sanctions, including German Ambassador Hahaner, Japanese Ambassador Sugimura, the Brazilian Ambassador, the ministers of Hungary and Austria, the Chargé d'Affaires of Albania, and their military attachés. (10th Havas Telegram)

(Rome) 60,000 soldiers of the army, fully armed, stood in front of the Palazzo Venezia at 8:00 p.m. last night. The officers were all wearing uniforms, gathering on the stone steps of the monument to the Unknown Soldier of the European War. Military songs and Fascist Party songs resonated with each other. The Prime Minister's residence and the statue of King Emmanuel I (Emmanuel I was the founder of the unified Kingdom of Italy) were illuminated by electric lights, as bright as day. Wounded soldiers who participated in the Italian-Abyssinian War were all dressed in colonial military uniforms. When the crowd saw them, they cheered and paid tribute. The railings of the balcony of the Palazzo Venezia were filled with Fascist Party flags. Envoys from all countries that did not participate in sanctions were invited to participate in the grand ceremony. Members of the Italian royal family also appeared on the balcony of the residence to watch. The scene was unprecedentedly grand. (10th Havas Telegram)

Trend of the League of Nations Meeting: Maintain Legal Relations with Abyssinia; Sanctions Against Italy Will Not Be Lifted 18

People from the League of Nations in Geneva recently declared that when the Administrative Council meets tomorrow, it will definitely refuse to file the fait accompli created by Italy, and maintain legal relations with the Abyssinian government. That is, the sanctions measures will probably not be lifted, because the legal status of a country can never be changed by the unilateral actions of other countries. The Abyssinian representative, that is, the Minister to France, Mr. Wold, is officially appointed by the Abyssinian government and has the right to represent the country at the Administrative Council. For example, when Germany occupied Belgium in 1914 and Austria occupied Serbia, this did not affect the legal status of Belgium and Serbia. The matter is exactly the same. (10th Havas Telegram)

(Geneva) The Administrative Council of the League of Nations is scheduled to hold a regular meeting tomorrow. In general, it is believed that the Council will postpone the discussion of various important issues, especially the Abyssinian and Rhineland issues. Spanish President Azana Elected, Election Results Announced Yesterday 31

Madrid The general election was held at the Crystal Palace at 10:45 am this morning and was completed at 12:15 pm this afternoon. The interim speaker of the House of Representatives, Jimenas, announced the election results at 2:00 pm this afternoon. Out of 847 votes, the incumbent Prime Minister Azana won the presidential election with 754 votes against 120 votes. (Havas, 10th)

Madrid The presidential election is scheduled to be held today. Half of the voters are members of the House of Representatives, and half are representatives of the national voters recently elected, a total of 925 people. Political figures predict that the incumbent Prime Minister Azana can be elected with a majority of 800 votes. The right-wing People's Action Party, the right-wing Catholic Party, and the Royalists, led by the former Landelino Lavilla Alsina, will vote against him. The left-wing Radical Party, led by Carballeiro, would rather Azana remain as Prime Minister. (Havas, 10th)

Madrid The new president, Azana, was born on January 1, 1880. He studied at a church school from an early age. After being admitted to the University of Madrid, he joined the famous Liberal Literary Research Association and organized the Restoration Party. In 1923, he joined the Republican Party and conspired to overthrow the late dictator General Rivera. In 1925, he recruited various Republicans and organized the "Civil Governance League." In 1930, he was elected as the chairman of the "Arden Valley Association" of the Republican faction and formed an alliance with the leaders of various Republican factions in San Sebastian to prepare for the revolution. He also organized a revolutionary committee and launched uprisings in the cities of Gallaecia and Madrid, but both failed. He then fled abroad. On April 14, 1931, after the revolution was completed, Azana took office as the Minister of the Army in the Zamora Cabinet and dismissed all the officers of the imperial faction. In the same year, he succeeded Zamora as Prime Minister. In August 1933, he resigned due to a vote of no confidence in the House of Representatives and took the position of leader of the opposition party. In 1934, the right-wing and central parties overthrew the government and seized power. Azana, as one of the key figures of the left wing, was immediately arrested and imprisoned. He was released soon after his imprisonment. After his release, he carried out anti-government movements and joined forces with the left-wing parties to organize the "People's Front." On February 16 of this year, the results of the general election of the House of Representatives showed that the left-wing parties had won a great victory. Azana then made a comeback and resumed his position as Prime Minister. Later, President Zamora was forced to resign, and the government decided to elect a successor president today, and he was elected president by an overwhelming majority. (Havas, 10th)

Taking Taiwan as a Major Base: Japan's Southern Advance Policy, Conspiratorial Activities in South China and Southeast Asia, Hoping to Achieve its Dream of Dominating East Asia 37

A special article from the Hualian News Agency: Since the occurrence of the North China Incident, it seems that the people of our country are not as concerned about the trend of the Japanese government's southern advance policy as they are about the mainland policy. This is a big mistake. Although Japan's offensive in North China is becoming increasingly urgent, its management in Taiwan, its conspiracies in South China, and its activities in various parts of Southeast Asia are all likely to cause serious situations. The Japanese government's ambition is to annex the entire China, control the weak nations along the Pacific coast, and fulfill its dream of dominating East Asia. The trend of its foreign policy, regardless of north or south, is closely related to the survival of our country and nation. He also recently announced a new marine policy, determined to actively develop in all directions of the South Pacific. At the same time, he is also very active in the provinces of South China, such as the activities of Japanese adventurers in Xiamen and the secret activities of Han traitor organizations in various counties in southern Fujian, all of which are directly or indirectly assisted by Taiwan. This is something that we must pay close attention to. As for the strengthening of the army and air force, efforts are also being made. The Taipei airport has been completed. The construction of this airport took seven months. The equipment is completely scientific, and its function is said to be the best in Japan. The keynote of the new naval policy recently announced by the Japanese government is completely consistent with the mainland policy of the Army Ministry, that is, to make the superiority of Southeast Asia a further preparation for dominating East Asia. The Japanese government's development towards Southeast Asia mainly targets Siam, Borneo, Malaya, the Philippines, and the Dutch East Indies, in order to confront the British and American navies and plunder natural resources. Therefore, the previous visit of Osami Nagano to the mandated islands was to plan for the establishment of defenses on the islands to cover the implementation of this marine policy. Japan's management of the Philippine Islands has not been a day or two. Currently, 60% of the land on Davao Island is owned by Japan, which shows the expansion of its power. The Japanese in the island intend to form a solid base as preparation for future wars. Therefore, the Filipinos said that it is possible to erupt a second "September 18th" incident, which is not unfounded. However, in the Japanese plan to dominate Southeast Asia, the management of the Philippine Islands is not a major task. Their current policy seems to be focused on the East Indian Islands and the Kra Isthmus of Siam. We all know that the East Indies are rich in natural resources, with oil reserves being the most abundant, which has long been coveted by the Japanese. But in addition to this, the Japanese also want to get involved in the island of New Guinea to cut off the connection between Hawaii and the Philippines. The second is the plan to cross the Kra Isthmus of Siam. In order to prosper Indochina and facilitate transportation with their own country, France once encouraged the Siamese government to carry out a canal digging plan, while Britain strongly opposed it due to military reasons, because if a canal is dug here, it will make Malaya a dead port. Now Japan is doing its best to contact Siam to promote its realization, and has repeatedly decided to send survey teams to carry out surveying and mapping in the name of studying geography, entomology or natural science, and has been trying to win over the Siamese government, hoping to eliminate the resistance of Britain and France, and carry out the excavation with Japanese capital assistance. Now a competition among Britain, France and Japan has been launched around this issue. Britain recently added 2 million pounds to its national defense expenditure to strengthen the defense preparations in Singapore, the target of which is nothing more than preparing for Japan's ambitions. In short, in the low-pressure Southeast Asia, Japan has the possibility of causing disputes anytime and anywhere. After Japan's decision to withdraw from the naval treaty and implement its marine policy, its future will become even more uncertain.

The Protagonist of the Assassination of Nagata Case: Lieutenant Colonel Aizawa Sentenced to Death, Disturbing Military Discipline is Unforgivable 39

(Tokyo) The case of Lieutenant Colonel Aizawa assassinating Lieutenant General Nagata, Director of the Military Affairs Bureau, in the Army Ministry, after the first trial of the first division was held on January 28 this year, ten consecutive trials were held. However, on February 26, the continued trial was suspended due to the outbreak of the incident. The authorities transferred the judge and renewed the trial. The first public trial was held on April 22. At the same time, all newspapers were prohibited from publishing news. At 11:30 p.m. on the 9th, the Army Ministry officially announced the following:

The case of Lieutenant Colonel Aizawa killing Lieutenant General Nagata was tried by the first division's military law conference. However, as a result of the outbreak of the rebellion incident, a part of the judges were replaced, and the case was retried. Five public trials have been held since April 22. However, the presiding judge believes that the debate in this case endangers the current order and military interests, and prohibits publicity. The trial continued, and the verdict was announced on May 7. On May 8, Lieutenant Colonel Aizawa appealed the verdict to the Army High Military Law Conference. The full text of the verdict is as follows:

"Aizawa Shiro, reserve army infantry lieutenant colonel, post-five rank, and the fourth class, former belongs to the Taiwan First Regiment, head of the family of samurai in No. 1, East Sixth Street, Sendai City, Miyagi Prefecture, is accompanied by the case of assaulting superior officer and murdering harm. The present Military Law Conference is prosecuted by Judge-Army Judge Shimada Tomosaburo, and the judgment is as follows: The defendant is sentenced to death, and the seized military sword is confiscated.

Summary of the Judgment Reason

(Tokyo) The summary of the Army Military Law Conference's judgment reason for Lieutenant Colonel Aizawa is as follows:

The defendant has always had a strong sense of respect for the emperor. Since Showa 4 (1929), he has recognized the necessity of the so-called Restoration, and his acquaintance with comrades such as Oishi Yoriyoshi, Okura Eiichi, Nishida Zei, Muranaka Koji, and Isobe Senichiro strengthened his belief. By Showa 8 (1933), he believed that in order to achieve the goal of the Showa Restoration, the national army should thoroughly understand the principle of the national polity. However, the current situation of the army runs counter to this. In March of Showa 9 (1934), Lieutenant General Nagata Tetsuzan took office as the Director of the Military Affairs Bureau. Based on the speeches of the aforementioned comrades, he believed that Lieutenant General Nagata used the name of controlling the military to obstruct the Showa Restoration. At that time, Infantry Captain Muranaka Koji and First Class Paymaster Ishikawa Asakazu were suspected of having a rebellion conspiracy and were suspended from their duties, and he believed that Director Nagata and others were scheming to harm his comrades, and was very angry. Also, in his post in Fukuyama City, he read the newspaper and learned that General Mazaki had resigned from the post of Education Director, and presumed that this was the result of Director Nagata's instigation. Therefore, he met Nagata and personally reported his resignation, but after learning that Nagata had no intention of resigning, he returned to Fukuyama. Not long after, after reading the strange document "The Rebellion of the Military Clique and Senior Ministers", he believed that the change of General Mazaki was an infringement of the supreme command, and decided to assassinate Director Nagata. Therefore, on August 11 of the tenth year, he came to Tokyo and stayed at Nishida Zei's house. After the meeting, he decided to carry out the assassination of Director Nagata. At 9:30 a.m. on the decided day (i.e., the 12th), he went to the Army Ministry, first entered the Director of the Maintenance Bureau's office to meet with Lieutenant General Yamaoka, and sent an aide to spy on Director Nagata in the office. At 9:45, he entered the Director of the Military Affairs Bureau's office and saw Director Nagata talking with Colonel Niimi Hideo, the commander of the Tokyo Military Police. He immediately threw the military sword he was wearing and slashed his back. The director fell beside the reception round table, and then slashed his head and stabbed his lungs several times, including the left side. Director Nagata died at 11:00 a.m. due to the knife wounds. When he added the first knife to Lieutenant General Nagata's back, seeing the colonel get up to stop him, Aizawa immediately injured his right upper arm. (10th day, Dentsu News Agency)

Talk from the Army Authorities

(Tokyo) The Army authorities issued a statement. The most regrettable point about this case is the destruction of military rules. Military rules are the lifeblood of the army. Lieutenant Colonel Aizawa assassinated his superior Lieutenant General Nagata, regardless of the reason, disturbed military rules, and the reason for his serious crime also exists in this. According to the court's deliberations on the cause of the crime, he generally believed in rumors and was based on his own self-righteous views. It is extremely regrettable that such a pure-hearted person was misled by strange documents. The army strictly maintains military discipline in order to eliminate such behavior. At the same time, it is necessary to thoroughly crack down on the strange documents that are the direct cause of this incident. Also, assassinating such public figures often has important behind-the-scenes relationships as usual. The world also holds such doubts about this incident. However, after the trial, it was clarified that there were no other accomplices. (10th day, Domei News Agency)

The Donations and Taxes for Enterprises Held in Various Provinces and Cities Should be Handled in Accordance with Legal Procedures 54

(Nanjing) Zhang Shuyong, chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Donation and Tax Supervision Committee, and others, submitted a letter to the Executive Yuan, saying that recently new policies have become increasingly complex, and most of the funding sources are not clearly defined. Local governments cannot cook without rice, so they set up various names to levy on the people, which is repeatedly burdensome and cannot be counted. The Central Government urged the abolition of exorbitant taxes and levies, and strives to implement it. Therefore, those who raise funds locally do not use the name of donations and taxes, but rather use certain expenses, believing that it does not involve the scope of donations and taxes, and can be free from legal restrictions. However, the funds contributed by the people, whether they are donations and taxes or expenses, are essentially the same. If this trend continues, after starting an enterprise and raising funds, arbitrary exactions will be made, and the people's strength will be unbearable. I am sincerely afraid that the benefits of the enterprise will not be developed, but the resources that can be exploited will be exhausted. It is a hindrance to both national planning and people's livelihood. After all, is the levy of taxes by local governments for the purpose of starting an enterprise, even if it is not called a donation or tax, should it be within the scope of donations and taxes, and can we be free from the restrictions of financial supervision laws? I have some doubts. After discussion, the people who were promoted and han asked your court to explain and instruct. If it is believed that it should be within the scope of donations and taxes, please order the provincial government to handle this kind of situation in accordance with legal procedures to show prudence. On the 23rd, according to Zhang Shuyong and others, the Executive Yuan notified all provinces and cities on the 9th that when a local government starts an enterprise and collects expenses, although it is not called a donation or tax, it is essentially no different from a donation or tax. It is true that you cannot avoid the name of donation or tax and be free from the restrictions of financial laws. At the same time, it also ordered the Ministry of Finance to comply. (10th day, Special Dispatch)
